I was looking for a billiards place that allowed minors (my youngest is 12) to enter and I found this place. Four of us got a table for $15/hr and we played a while and had a great time. It wasn't crowded at all, music played all the while, and it wad a lot of fun. The tables are good. I don't remember if they serve food but some packaged snacks are available. We will definitely return.</review>

Had an initial shipping snafu, called to clear things up, had a message sent to the local UPS center, had a call back in under 5 minutes, cleared things up and got my package back on track.

In reading one star reviews I get the feeling that some people don't understand the complexities involved in shipping, tracking, and delivering millions of packages daily. In two plus decades of shipping, I've never lost a package or had an issue that couldn't be resolved with a few phone calls. The same applies to FedEx.

WARNING: OneTrac is hands down the worst delivery company. Maybe a solid 3 out of 10 in war torn Syria but an abysmal failure in America.< /text>

<Rate>4<//Rate><Text>Cute, quiet Poke place with lots of open space. Service was ok and the food was not bad. You can build your own bowl, or they had 2 popular options for you to choose from. I decided to build my own 3 scoop poke, for $11 (appx pre-tax). I had salmon, shoyu tuna and scallops. They also had a spicy tuna choice and a couple others. Toppings again were more limited than other poke places I've been to, but not bad and sauce variety was ok as well. I added lemon-yuzu and shoyu into my bowl, as well as unagi, ponzu and a spicy mayo sauce to top it all off (yes, I like my food saucy). You can have all of that on top of white rice (not sushi rice... booo), brown rice or a salad. Over all the portion was decent and toppings were ok, so I'd say it's pretty average.

However, their supreme masubi was pretty darn good (saucy, you see a pattern?). haha I liked it a lot and would definitely recommend trying it, if you like more flavorful spam masubis.<//Text><pictures>None< /pictures>< Response>
None</Response>

<Name>Sandra Self< /Name><pics>None<//pics><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
Dear Dr. Smith and Staff,

The words I cannot begin to describe in full how I feel about Dr. Smith, his staff and office. They are so totally awesome, kind, patient, helpful and understanding and that is only a little part of what I have to say.

I called at the very last minute to get an apt. scheduled before the year was up so I could maximize all my benefits. They came in on their day off to take care of me and several others that were in the same situation.

First you have to understand I am deathly afraid of going to a dentist office.  Second I have Fibromyalgia with chronic fatigue and I am in pain all the time. Third I have a hard time getting numb and I am not easily sedated.

With all of this going on I have had to walk a very long road in trying to get help, being passed up & spit out like I did not exist. I have spent the last year eating only soft foods because of the work done on me at my last two dental appointments. Needless to say it has not been a easy road.

I was VERY VERY worried that I was going to go thru the same thing as before (pain, not being sedated right & coming out with a worse problem then I went in for) but that was not the case. Not only did they fit me in, they spoke with me about the work that needed to be done, they showed me the X-Rays and explained the problem areas I had.

On the day of my procedure I do not remember anything from the time they started my IV until 5 PM that evening. I did not wake up or either do not remember waking up if I did during the procedure. I was so relaxed I slept like a baby and anyone who knows anything about Fibromyalgia knows we do not sleep, we are in pain 24/7, we are tense and fatigued and things do not work on us like they do on the average person and last we do not sedate easily.

Dr. Smith has been the only dentist that has ever been able to sedate me the way he did and for that I am very thankful for. He called my house that same evening after the procedure to check how I was doing.

I have finally found a Dentist who understands what I go thru and who can deal with my difficulties. His work is superb, even thou I still have a lot more work that needs to be done I have my smile back and I am starting to eat real food again because of him and for that I am so very thankful.

On another note behind every good Doctor there is a great team of people working with him. I was surrounded by his staff as if I was the only person in the room, they were all making me feel comfortable while doing their job.

There is one particular person her name is Melissa, she is the one who took my X-Rays and initial report on me and she did an absolutely fantastic job in making me comfortable and totally understood when I could not hold the object in my mouth she found another alternative to help me finish the X-Rays. She also allowed me to talk about my previous events that I had dealt with. I felt like finally someone is actually listening to what I was saying and they cared about trying to do what they could to help me. Afterwards she went and told the Doctor about me and the work I needed and my financial problems. The Doctor then came in and spoke with me about everything. All I can say is I felt like I was at home surrounded by family and that I have never felt before at any dental office I have visited in my life time.

There is not one complaint that I can make. I only wish I would of found them sooner.

Thank you so much

Sincerely

Sandra Self<//Review>

<review>This is an outstanding jewelry repair shop with superior customer service and reception by Eunise, who carefully inspects each piece to be repaired and consults with Mike the in house expert for the cost estimate and time frame for repair. The pricing is fair and a good value for the quality of work. Cleaning of jewelry is also available and my individual pieces were restored to new gleaming luster.

Mike is a seasoned tradesman with a myriad of skills in watch repair, horologist, gemology, silversmith, diamond setter and jewelry knowledge and talent that is at the highest professional standards of his craft.

Fast-Fix is a hidden gem. They are independently owned and operated and with this particular location, a pride of ownership is shown, with professional etiquette, value and superior quality of work.

Highly recommend!<//review><Pictures>None</Pictures><Resp>None</Resp>< gmap_id>
